DeleteResponse, err error) {\n\ttxn := k.KV.Txn(ctx).If(\n\t\tclientv3.Compare(clientv3.ModRevision(key), \"=\", expectedRevision),\n\t).Then(\n\t\tclientv3.OpDelete(key),\n\t)\n\tif opts.GetOnFailure
